msg:The hotel's services, facilities and food are all very good, so I won't say much. I'll just give you a small suggestion for your reference. Double rooms are occupied by two people, and their activities are unlikely to be completely synchronized. Sometimes one person is out while the other is in the room, so one door magnetic card is not enough. Although you can go to the front desk to get another one, it is always inconvenient, so it is recommended to have at least two door magnetic cards for multi-person rooms.
